Task instruction sent to agent 
# Envoy xDS v2 to v3 API Migration

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement both xDS v2 and v3 API handling: the versioned proto type conversion, the v2-to-v3 field renames (e.g., DiscoveryRequest), and the dual-version subscription handling in the ADS gRPC server.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

    13→
    14→// A service's name, e.g. "envoy.api.v2.RouteDiscoveryService",
    15→// "envoy.service.route.v3.RouteDiscoveryService".
    16→using ServiceName = std::string;
    17→
    18→// A resource type URL. For example: "type.googleapis.com/envoy.api.v2.RouteConfiguration".
    19→using TypeUrl = std::string;
    20→
    21→TypeUrl getResourceTypeUrl(absl::string_view service_name) {
    22→  const auto* service_desc = Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindServiceByName(
    23→      static_cast<ServiceName>(service_name));
    24→  ASSERT(service_desc != nullptr, fmt::format("{} missing", service_name));
    25→  ASSERT(service_desc->options().HasExtension(envoy::annotations::resource));
    26→
    27→  return Grpc::Common::typeUrl(
    28→      service_desc->options().GetExtension(envoy::annotations::resource).type());
    29→}

    13→// process handles a bi-di stream request
    14→func (s *server) processADS(sw *streamWrapper, reqCh chan *discovery.DiscoveryRequest) error {
    15→	// Create a buffered multiplexed channel the size of the known resource types.
    16→	respChan := make(chan cache.Response, types.UnknownType)
    17→
    18→	// Instead of creating a separate channel for each incoming request and abandoning the old one
    19→	// This algorithm uses (and reuses) a single channel for all request types and guarantees
    20→	// the server will send updates over the wire in an ordered fashion.
    21→	// Downside is there is no longer back pressure per resource.
    22→	// There is potential for a dropped response from the cache but this is not impactful
    23→	// to the client since SOTW version handling is global and a new sequence will be
    24→	// initiated on a new request.
    25→	processAllExcept := func(typeURL string) error {
    26→		for {
    27→			select {
    28→			// We watch the multiplexed ADS channel for incoming responses.
    29→			case res := <-respChan:
    30→				if res.GetRequest().GetTypeUrl() != typeURL {
    31→					if err := sw.send(res); err != nil {
    32→						return err
    33→					}
    34→				}
    35→			default:
    36→				return nil
    37→			}
    38→		}
    39→	}
    40→
    41→	// This control loop strictly orders reso
... (truncated)

package envoy.service.discovery.v2;

import "envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto";

import "udpa/annotations/status.proto";

option java_package = "io.envoyproxy.envoy.service.discovery.v2";
option java_outer_classname = "AdsProto";
option java_multiple_files = true;
option go_package = "github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/service/discovery/v2;discoveryv2";
option (udpa.annotations.file_status).package_version_status = FROZEN;

// [#protodoc-title: Aggregated Discovery Service (ADS)]

// Discovery services for endpoints, clusters, routes,
// and listeners are retained in the package `envoy.api.v2` for backwards
// compatibility with existing management servers. New development in discovery
// services should proceed in the package `envoy.service.discovery.v2`.

// See https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy-api#apis for a description of the role of
// ADS and how it is intended to be used by a management server. ADS requests
// have the same structure as their singleton xDS counterparts, but can
// multiplex many resource types on a single stream. The type_url in the
// DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse provides sufficient information to recover
// the multiplexed singleton APIs at the Envoy instance and management server.
service AggregatedDiscoveryService {
  // This is a gRPC-only API.
  rpc StreamAggregatedResources(stream api.v2.DiscoveryRequest)
      returns (stream api.v2.DiscoveryResponse) {
  }

  rpc DeltaAggregatedResources(stream api.v2.DeltaDiscoveryRequest)
      returns (stream api.v2.DeltaDiscoveryResponse) {
  }
}

// [#not-implemented-hide:] Not configuration. Workaround c++ protobuf issue with importing
// services: https://github.com/google/protobuf/issues/4221
message AdsDummy {
}

// [#protodoc-title: Common discovery API components]

// A DiscoveryRequest requests a set of versioned resources of the same type for
// a given Envoy node on some API.
// [#next-free-field: 7]
message DiscoveryRequest {
  // The version_info provided in the request messages will be the version_info
  // received with the most recent successfully processed response or empty on
  // the first request. It is expected that no new request is sent after a
  // response is received until the Envoy instance is ready to ACK/NACK the new
  // configuration. ACK/NACK takes place by returning the new API config version
  // as applied or the previous API config version respectively. Each type_url
  // (see below) has an independent version associated with it.
  string version_info = 1;

  // The node making the request.
  core.Node node = 2;

  // List of resources to subscribe to, e.g. list of cluster names or a route
  // configuration name. If this is empty, all resources for the API are
  // returned. LDS/CDS may have empty resource_names, which will cause all
  // resources for the Envoy instance to be returned. The LDS and CDS responses
  // will then imply a number of reso

package envoy.service.discovery.v3;

// [#protodoc-title: Common discovery API components]

// Specifies a resource to be subscribed to.
message ResourceLocator {
  // The resource name to subscribe to.
  string name = 1;

  // A set of dynamic parameters used to match against the dynamic parameter
  // constraints on the resource. This allows clients to select between
  // multiple variants of the same resource.
  map<string, string> dynamic_parameters = 2;
}

// Specifies a concrete resource name.
message ResourceName {
  // The name of the resource.
  string name = 1;

  // Dynamic parameter constraints associated with this resource. To be used by client-side caches
  // (including xDS proxies) when matching subscribed resource locators.
  DynamicParameterConstraints dynamic_parameter_constraints = 2;
}

// [#not-implemented-hide:]
// An error associated with a specific resource name, returned to the
// client by the server.
message ResourceError {
  // The name of the resource.
  ResourceName resource_name = 1;

  // The error reported for the resource.
  google.rpc.Status error_detail = 2;
}

   150→  /**
   151→   * Validate transport_api_version field in ApiConfigSource.
   152→   * @param api_config_source the config source to extract transport API version from.
   153→   * @returns a failure status when the transport version is disabled.
   154→   */
   155→  template <class Proto> static absl::Status checkTransportVersion(const Proto& api_config_source) {
   156→    const auto transport_api_version = api_config_source.transport_api_version();
   157→    ASSERT_IS_MAIN_OR_TEST_THREAD();
   158→    if (transport_api_version != envoy::config::core::v3::ApiVersion::AUTO &&
   159→        transport_api_version != envoy::config::core::v3::ApiVersion::V3) {
   160→      const std::string& warning = fmt::format(
   161→          "V2 xDS transport protocol version is deprecated in {}. "
   162→          "The v2 xDS major version has been removed and is no longer supported. "
   163→          "See the advice in https://www.envoyproxy.io/docs/envoy/latest/faq/api/envoy_v3.",
   164→          api_config_source.DebugString());
   165→      ENVOY_LOG_MISC(warn, warning);
   166→      return absl::InvalidArgumentError(warning);
   167→    }
   168→    return absl::OkStatus();
   169→  }
   170→

   464→void MessageUtil::unpackToOrThrow(const ProtobufWkt::Any& any_message, Protobuf::Message& message) {
   465→#if defined(ENVOY_ENABLE_FULL_PROTOS)
   466→  if (!any_message.UnpackTo(&message)) {
   467→    throwEnvoyExceptionOrPanic(fmt::format("Unable to unpack as {}: {}",
   468→                                           message.GetDescriptor()->full_name(),
   469→                                           any_message.DebugString()));
   470→#else
   471→  if (!message.ParseFromString(any_message.value())) {
   472→    throwEnvoyExceptionOrPanic(
   473→        fmt::format("Unable to unpack as {}: {}", message.GetTypeName(), any_message.type_url()));
   474→#endif
   475→  }
   476→}
   477→
   478→absl::Status MessageUtil::unpackTo(const ProtobufWkt::Any& any_message,
   479→                                   Protobuf::Message& message) {
   480→#if defined(ENVOY_ENABLE_FULL_PROTOS)
   481→  if (!any_message.UnpackTo(&message)) {
   482→    return absl::InternalError(absl::StrCat("Unable to unpack as ",
   483→                                            message.GetDescriptor()->full_name(), ": ",
   484→                                            any_message.DebugString()));
   485→#else
   486→  if (!message.ParseFromString(any_message.value())) {
   487→    return absl::InternalError(
   488→        absl::StrCat("Unable to unpack as ", message.GetTypeName(), ": ", any_message.type_url()));
   489→#endif
   490→  }
   491→  // Ok Status is returned if `UnpackTo` succeeded.
   492→  return absl::OkStatus();
   493→}

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key C++ Source Files in envoyproxy/envoy for xDS v2→v3 Migration

### Versioned Proto Type Conversion & Field Renames
- **`api/envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto`** — v2 `DiscoveryRequest` (package `envoy.api.v2`)
- **`api/envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.proto`** — v3 `DiscoveryRequest` annotated with `previous_message_type = "envoy.api.v2.DiscoveryRequest"`
- **`api/envoy/service/discovery/v2/ads.proto`** and **`v3/ads.proto`** — the actual v2/v3 ADS service definitions

### Dual-Version Subscription Handling (ADS gRPC)
| File | Description |
|------|-------------|
| `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.cc` | SotW ADS (`DiscoveryRequest`/`DiscoveryResponse`) via `StreamAggregatedResources` |
| `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.cc` | Delta ADS (`DeltaDiscoveryRequest`) via `DeltaAggregatedResources` |
| `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc` | Unified mux templated for both SotW (`GrpcMuxSotw`) and Delta (`GrpcMuxDelta`) |
| `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc` | SotW state machine handling `DiscoveryResponse`/`DiscoveryRequest` |
| `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc` | Delta state machine |

### Version Enforcement & Type Mapping
- **`source/common/config/utility.h`** — `checkTransportVersion()` rejects v2 transport API version
- **`source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc`** — maps resource type URLs to `sotwGrpcMethod`/`deltaGrpcMethod` v3 service methods (with v2 naming documented in comments)
- **`source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc`** — orchestrates SotW vs Delta mux selection

We build a reverse map from resource type URL to\n  // service methods (versioned by transport_api_version). We explicitly enumerate all services,\n  // since DescriptorPool doesn't support iterating over all descriptors, due its lazy load design,\n  // see https://www.mail-archive.com/protobuf@googlegroups.com/msg04540.html.\n  for (absl::string_view name : {\n           \"envoy.service.route.v3.RouteDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.route.v3.ScopedRoutesDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.route.v3.ScopedRoutesDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.route.v3.VirtualHostDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.secret.v3.SecretDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.cluster.v3.ClusterDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.endpoint.v3.EndpointDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.endpoint.v3.LocalityEndpointDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.listener.v3.ListenerDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.runtime.v3.RuntimeDiscoveryService\",\n           \"envoy.service.extension.v3.ExtensionConfigDiscoveryService\",\n       }) {\n    const TypeUrl resource_type_url = getResourceTypeUrl(name);\n    V3Service& service = (*type_url_to_versioned_service_map)[resource_type_url];\n\n    const auto* service_desc =\n        Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindServiceByName(std::string(name));\n    ASSERT(service_desc != nullptr, fmt::format(\"{} missing\", name));\n    ASSERT(service_desc->options().HasExtension(envoy::annotations::resource));\n\n    // We populate the service methods that are known below, but it's possible that some\n    // services don't implement all, e.g. VHDS doesn't support SotW or REST.\n    for (int method_index = 0; method_index < service_desc->method_count(); ++method_index) {\n      const auto& method_desc = *service_desc->method(method_index);\n      if (absl::StartsWith(method_desc.name(), \"Stream\")) {\n        service.sotw_grpc_ = method_desc.full_name();\n      } else if (absl::StartsWith(method_desc.name(), \"Delta\")) {\n        service.delta_grpc_ = method_desc.full_name();\n      } else if (absl::StartsWith(method_desc.name(), \"Fetch\")) {\n        service.rest_ = method_desc.full_name();\n      } else {\n        ASSERT(false, \"Unknown xDS service method\");\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  return type_url_to_versioned_service_map;\n}\n\nTypeUrlToV3ServiceMap& typeUrlToV3ServiceMap() {\n  static TypeUrlToV3ServiceMap* type_url_to_versioned_service_map = buildTypeUrlToServiceMap();\n  return *type_url_to_versioned_service_map;\n}\n\n} // namespace\n\nconst Protobuf::MethodDescriptor& deltaGrpcMethod(absl::string_view type_url) {\n  const auto it = typeUrlToV3ServiceMap().find(static_cast<TypeUrl>(type_url));\n  ASSERT(it != typeUrlToV3ServiceMap().cend());\n  return *Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindMethodByName(it->second.delta_grpc_);\n}\n\nconst Protobuf::MethodDescriptor& sotwGrpcMethod(absl::string_view type_url) {\n  const auto it = typeUrlToV3ServiceMap().find(static_cast<TypeUrl>(type_url));\n  ASSERT(it != typeUrlToV3ServiceMap().cend());\n  return *Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindMethodByName(it->second.sotw_grpc_);\n}\n\nconst Protobuf::MethodDescriptor& restMethod(absl::string_view type_url) {\n  const auto it = typeUrlToV3ServiceMap().find(static_cast<TypeUrl>(type_url));\n  ASSERT(it != typeUrlToV3ServiceMap().cend());\n  return *Protobuf::DescriptorPool::generated_pool()->FindMethodByName(it->second.rest_);\n}\n\n} // namespace Config\n} // namespace Envoy\n",

Versioned Proto Type Conversion and Field Renames (DiscoveryRequest)**\\nThe proto files in `api/envoy/api/v2/discovery.proto` define the original v2 `DiscoveryRequest` (in package `envoy.api.v2`), while `api/envoy/service/discovery/v3/discovery.proto` defines the v3 `DiscoveryRequest` (in package `envoy.service.discovery.v3`) with the UDPA annotation `option (udpa.annotations.versioning).previous_message_type = \\\"envoy.api.v2.DiscoveryRequest\\\"` documenting the rename. The v2 ADS service is defined in `api/envoy/service/discovery/v2/ads.proto` (using `envoy.api.v2.DiscoveryRequest`), and the v3 equivalent in `api/envoy/service/discovery/v3/ads.proto` (using `envoy.service.discovery.v3.DiscoveryRequest`).\\n\\n**2. Dual-Version Subscription Handling in the ADS gRPC Client**\\nThe Envoy proxy acts as an xDS client against an external management server. Two independent implementations handle the ADS gRPC protocol:\\n- **SotW (State of the World)** \u2014 the original v2 model using `DiscoveryRequest`/`DiscoveryResponse`: implemented in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.cc` (`GrpcMuxImpl` class), which calls `envoy.service.discovery.v3.AggregatedDiscoveryService.StreamAggregatedResources`.\\n- **Delta xDS** \u2014 the v3 extension using `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`/`DeltaDiscoveryResponse`: implemented in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.cc` (`NewGrpcMuxImpl`), which calls `DeltaAggregatedResources`.\\n\\nA unified implementation in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc` provides `GrpcMuxSotw` and `GrpcMuxDelta` as template instantiations of a single `GrpcMuxImpl<S,F,RQ,RS>`, covering both `envoy::service::discovery::v3::DiscoveryRequest` (SotW) and `envoy::service::discovery::v3::DeltaDiscoveryRequest` (Delta) within one templated class.\\n\\nThe corresponding per-subscription state machines are:\\n- `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc` \u2014 `SotwSubscriptionState`, handles `DiscoveryResponse` and builds `DiscoveryRequest` ACK/NACKs with `version_info` and `response_nonce`.\\n- `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc` \u2014 `DeltaSubscriptionState`, handles `DeltaDiscoveryResponse` and builds `DeltaDiscoveryRequest`.\\n- `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/delta_subscription_state.cc` \u2014 original (non-unified) delta state used by `NewGrpcMuxImpl`.\\n\\n**3. Type URL to gRPC Service Method Mapping**\\n`source/common/config/type_to_endpoint.cc` builds a reverse map from v3 resource type URLs (e.g. `type.googleapis.com/envoy.config.cluster.v3.Cluster`) to the correct v3 gRPC service methods (`sotwGrpcMethod`, `deltaGrpcMethod`, `restMethod`).
